<file>
remake/src/renderer/RenderLayer.ts

**Summary:**
Task-R4。Babylon.js RenderingGroupId 分层系统，4 层深度排序。

**Key elements:**
- `RenderLayer` enum：Opaque=0, Transparent=1, Sprite=2, Overlay=3
- `setRenderLayer(mesh, layer)`：设置 mesh.renderingGroupId
- `getRenderLayer(mesh)`：读取当前层
- `getRenderLayerStats(scene)`：统计各层 mesh 数量

**Latest version:**
```ts
export enum RenderLayer { Opaque = 0, Transparent = 1, Sprite = 2, Overlay = 3 }
export const RENDER_LAYER_COUNT = 4;

export function setRenderLayer(mesh: { renderingGroupId: number }, layer: RenderLayer): void {
  mesh.renderingGroupId = layer;
}
export function getRenderLayer(mesh: { renderingGroupId: number }): RenderLayer {
  return (mesh.renderingGroupId ?? 0) as RenderLayer;
}
export function getRenderLayerStats(scene: { meshes: ReadonlyArray<{ renderingGroupId: number }> }): Record<number, number> {
  const stats: Record<number, number> = { 0: 0, 1: 0, 2: 0, 3: 0 };
  for (const m of scene.meshes) stats[m.renderingGroupId ?? 0]++;
  return stats;
}
```
</file>

<file>
remake/src/game/traits/Trait.ts

**Summary:**
Task-C2。在原有 Trait 基类上新增 ConditionalTrait 和 UpgradeableTrait，以及 IObservesVariables 条件观察接口。

**Key elements:**
- `IObservesVariables`：条件变化时回调 `onConditionChanged(actor, condition, active)`
- `ConditionalTrait extends Trait`：`requiredConditions: string[]`，`isEnabled(actor)` 检查条件，`tickEnabled()` 仅在启用时执行
- `UpgradeableTrait<T>`：`baseValue` / `upgradedValue`，`getCurrentValue(actor)` 根据条件返回不同值
- `TraitRegistry.sortTypes()`：Kahn 拓扑排序（A4）

**Latest version:**
```ts
export interface IObservesVariables {
  onConditionChanged(actor: Actor, condition: string, active: boolean): void;
}

export abstract class ConditionalTrait extends Trait {
  abstract readonly requiredConditions: readonly string[];
  private enabled = false;

  isEnabled(actor: Actor): boolean {
    if (this.requiredConditions.length === 0) return true;
    return this.requiredConditions.every((c) => actor.hasCondition(c));
  }

  override tick(actor: Actor, deltaTime: number): void {
    const shouldBeEnabled = this.isEnabled(actor);
    if (shouldBeEnabled !== this.enabled) this.enabled = shouldBeEnabled;
    if (this.enabled) this.tickEnabled(actor, deltaTime);
  }
  tickEnabled(_actor: Actor, _deltaTime: number): void {}
}

export abstract class UpgradeableTrait<T> extends Trait {
  constructor(private baseValue: T, private upgradedValue: T) { super(); }
  private upgradeCondition: string | null = null;
  setUpgradeCondition(c: string | null): void { this.upgradeCondition = c; }
  getCurrentValue(actor: Actor): T {
    return (this.upgradeCondition && actor.hasCondition(this.upgradeCondition)) ? this.upgradedValue : this.baseValue;
  }
}
```
</file>

<file>
remake/src/game/actors/Actor.ts

**Summary:**
Task-C1/C2。Actor 条件管理 + 条件变化通知观察者。

**Key elements:**
- `conditions: Map<string, number>` 条件计数器
- `grantCondition(condition): number` 返回 token，`revokeCondition(token)` 撤销
- `notifyConditionChanged()` 内部方法：遍历所有 Trait，通知 `IObservesVariables` / `ConditionalTrait` / `UpgradeableTrait`

**Latest version（条件相关片段）：**
```ts
export class Actor {
  private conditions = new Map<string, number>();
  private nextConditionToken = 1;

  grantCondition(condition: string): number {
    const token = this.nextConditionToken++;
    this.conditions.set(condition, (this.conditions.get(condition) ?? 0) + 1);
    this.notifyConditionChanged(condition, true);
    return token;
  }

  revokeCondition(token: number): void {
    // 查找并移除 token 对应的条件（简化映射查找）
    // ... 省略实现 ...
    this.notifyConditionChanged(condition, false);
  }

  hasCondition(condition: string): boolean {
    return (this.conditions.get(condition) ?? 0) > 0;
  }

  private notifyConditionChanged(condition: string, active: boolean): void {
    for (const trait of this.traits) {
      if (isObservesVariables(trait)) trait.onConditionChanged(this, condition, active);
      if (trait instanceof ConditionalTrait || trait instanceof UpgradeableTrait) {
        trait.onConditionChanged(this, condition, active);
      }
    }
  }
}
```
</file>

remake/src/assets/loaders/ShpTextureBuilder.ts

**Summary:**
Task-SPR3。SHP 文件解析 → HTML Canvas 纹理图集，含 RLE 解压和 UV 坐标生成。

**Key elements:**
- `ShpTextureBuilder.build(buffer)`：解析 TS/RA1 格式 SHP，返回 `{ canvas, frames[], atlasWidth, atlasHeight }`
- `decodeRleFrame()`：TS 格式 RLE 解压（0x00 透明跳过，0xxx 直接写入）
- `buildAtlas()`：网格布局所有帧到 canvas，生成 UV 坐标（Babylon Y-flip）
- 返回 `AtlasFrame { u, v, u2, v2, width, height }`

**Latest version（关键逻辑）：**
```ts
export interface AtlasFrame { u: number; v: number; u2: number; v2: number; width: number; height: number; }

export const ShpTextureBuilder = {
  build(buffer: ArrayBuffer): { canvas: HTMLCanvasElement; frames: AtlasFrame[]; atlasWidth: number; atlasHeight: number } | null {
    const info = ShpLoader.parse(buffer);
    if (!info.isValid || info.frames.length === 0) return null;
    const frames = info.frames.map((f, i) => this.decodeFrame(buffer, f, i));
    return this.buildAtlas(frames);
  },

  decodeFrame(buffer: ArrayBuffer, frame: ShpFrame, _index: number): Uint8ClampedArray {
    // TS format RLE decode: dataOffset + 24 header, read until 0x00 sentinel
    // RA1 fallback: raw copy
    // returns RGBA pixel data
  },

  buildAtlas(frames: Uint8ClampedArray[]): { canvas: HTMLCanvasElement; frames: AtlasFrame[]; atlasWidth: number; atlasHeight: number } {
    // 网格布局，canvas 2D putImageData，计算 UV（v flipped for Babylon）
  }
};
```

remake/src/game/unit/AircraftTrait.ts

**Summary:**
Task-VEH1。Actor/Trait 架构下的 Aircraft 飞行逻辑 + 机场 Reservable 停泊系统。

**Key elements:**
- `AircraftTrait extends Trait`：`cruiseAltitude`, `landAltitude`, `canHover`, `state`（Idle/TakeOff/Cruise/Land）
- `flyTo(targetX, targetY)`：设置飞行目标，自动状态转换
- `updatePosition(dt)`：每 tick 更新位置，到达目标后切换状态
- `Reservable`：机场停机位管理，`totalSlots`, `reserve(aircraftId)`, `release(aircraftId)`, `getReservation(aircraftId)`

**Latest version（关键逻辑）：**
```ts
export enum AircraftState { Idle = 'Idle', TakeOff = 'TakeOff', Cruise = 'Cruise', Land = 'Land' }

export class AircraftTrait extends Trait {
  cruiseAltitude = 15;
  landAltitude = 0.5;
  canHover = false;
  state = AircraftState.Idle;
  private targetX = 0;
  private targetY = 0;

  flyTo(tx: number, ty: number): void {
    this.targetX = tx; this.targetY = ty;
    this.state = AircraftState.TakeOff;
  }

  override tick(actor: Actor, _deltaTime: number): void {
    if (this.state === AircraftState.Cruise || this.state === AircraftState.TakeOff) {
      this.updatePosition(actor);
    }
  }

  private updatePosition(actor: Actor): void {
    const dx = this.targetX - actor.x;
    const dy = this.targetY - actor.y;
    const dist = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
    if (dist < 0.5) { this.state = AircraftState.Idle; return; }
    const speed = 0.3;
    actor.x += (dx / dist) * speed;
    actor.y += (dy / dist) * speed;
    if (this.state === AircraftState.TakeOff && Math.abs(actor.y - this.targetY) < 5) {
      this.state = AircraftState.Cruise;
    }
  }
}

export class Reservable {
  private slots = new Map<string, string>(); // slotIndex -> aircraftId
  constructor(readonly totalSlots: number) {}
  reserve(aircraftId: string): number { /* 找空闲 slot，返回索引或 -1 */ }
  release(aircraftId: string): void { /* 释放 */ }
  getReservation(aircraftId: string): number { /* 返回 slot 索引或 -1 */ }
}
```

   167	---
   168	
   169	## 3. WorldActor 与全局系统（🟡 P1）
   170	
   171	### 3.1 现状
   172	
   173	全局系统为独立单例：
   174	- `ActorMap` 单例
   175	- `ScreenMap` 未实现
   176	- `SelectionManager` 单例
   177	- `FogOfWar` 单例
   178	- `BulletManager` 单例
   179	
   180	### 3.2 OpenRA 设计
   181	
   182	```csharp
   183	// WorldActor 是一个特殊 Actor，挂载所有世界级 Trait
   184	var worldActor = new Actor(world, "world");
   185	worldActor.AddTrait(new ActorMap(worldActor, world));
   186	worldActor.AddTrait(new ScreenMap(worldActor, world));
   187	worldActor.AddTrait(new Selection(worldActor, world));
   188	worldActor.AddTrait(new ControlGroups(worldActor, world));
   189	
   190	// 这些 Trait 通过 WorldActor 参与正常 tick/render 生命周期
   191	```
   192	
   193	### 3.3 差距分析
   194	
   195	- 单例模式难以支持多世界/多房间场景
   196	- `WorldActor` 模式将所有系统纳入统一生命周期管理
   197	- 便于 mod 替换（如自定义 `ActorMap` 实现）
   198	
   199	### 3.4 改进任务
   200	
   201	- [x] **Task-W1: WorldActor 引入** ✅ 2026-05-28
   202	  - `World` 类创建时初始化 `worldActor: Actor`
   203	  - 将 `ActorMap`、`FogOfWar`、`SelectionManager` 等改造为 Trait 并挂载到 `worldActor`
   204	  - `World.Tick()` 时 `worldActor.tick()` 参与正常遍历
   205	  - 删除对应单例，通过 `world.worldActor.trait<ActorMap>()` 访问
   206

     1	import { LandType } from '../terrain/TerrainGrid';
     2	import { Locomotion } from './UnitDefinitions';
     3	
     4	/**
     5	 * OpenRA-style Locomotor configuration.
     6	 *
     7	 * Mirrors `OpenRA.Mods.Common/Traits/Mobile.cs` → `LocomotorInfo`.
     8	 * Each locomotion class (Foot / Track / Wheel / Winged / Float) defines
     9	 * how units of that type interact with terrain and other actors.
    10	 *
    11	 * Source: OpenRA/OpenRA.Mods.Common/Traits/Mobile.cs, LocomotorInfo class
    12	 */
    13	export interface LocomotorInfo {
    14	  /** Human-readable name (e.g. "Foot", "Track"). */
    15	  readonly name: string;
    16	
    17	  /** Average wait time when blocked (milliseconds). */
    18	  readonly waitAverage: number;
    19	
    20	  /** Spread added to wait time to desync multiple units (milliseconds). */
    21	  readonly waitSpread: number;
    22	
    23	  /** Whether multiple units of this locomotor can share the same cell. */
    24	  readonly sharesCell: boolean;
    25	
    26	  /**
    27	   * Terrain speed modifiers.
    28	   * Key = LandType, value = speed multiplier (0 = impassable).
    29	   * The A* edge cost is computed as `distance / terrainSpeed`.
    30	   */
    31	  readonly terrainSpeeds: Readonly<Record<LandType, number>>;
    32	
    33	  /**
    34	   * Maximum turn speed in degrees per second.
    35	   * Heavy tanks (Track) turn slowly and may need to stop to turn.
    36	   * Light vehicles (Wheel) turn quickly while moving.
    37	   */
    38	  readonly turnSpeed: number;
    39	
    40	  /**
    41	   * Whether the unit can turn while moving.
    42	   * false = must stop at cell boundary, rotate in place, then resume.
    43	   * true = rotates smoothly while interpolating between cells.
    44	   */
    45	  readonly turnsWhileMoving: boolean;
    46	
    47	  /**
    48	   * Actor categories this locomotor can crush (e.g. `["infantry"]`).
    49	   * Empty array = cannot crush anything.
    50	   */
    51	  readonly crushes: readonly string[];
    52	}
    53	
    54	/**
    55	 * Pre-defined locomotor definitions matching classic C&C behavior.
    56	 *
    57	 * Foot:   infantry — can share cells, slow on rough terrain, can squeeze through rocks.
    58	 * Track:  tracked vehicles — cannot share cells, blocked by rocks.
    59	 * Wheel:  wheeled vehicles — cannot share cells, blocked by rocks, faster on roads.
    60	 * Winged: aircraft — flies over everything.
    61	 * Float:  naval — only water/beach/river.
    62	 */

   124	    },
   125	  },
   126

   128	    name: 'Winged',
   129	    waitAverage: 200,
   130	    waitSpread: 100,
   131	    sharesCell: false,
   132	    turnSpeed: 360,
   133	    turnsWhileMoving: true,
   134	    crushes: [],

   136	      [LandType.Clear]: 1,
   137	      [LandType.Road]: 1,
   138	      [LandType.Water]: 1,
   139	      [LandType.Rock]: 1,

   164	      [LandType.Rough]: 0,
   165	      [LandType.River]: 1,
   166	    },
   167	  },
   168	};
   169	
   170	/** Look up the locomotor definition for a given locomotion enum value. */
   171	export function getLocomotor(locomotion: Locomotion): LocomotorInfo {
   172	  return LOCOMOTOR_DEFINITIONS[locomotion];
   173	}
   174	
   175	/**
   176	 * Create a terrain-cost callback for a specific locomotor.
   177	 *
   178	 * The callback queries the terrain type at (x, y) and returns the
   179	 * locomotor's speed modifier for that terrain (0 = impassable).
   180	 *
   181	 * This callback is passed to `Pathfinder.findPath()` so that A*
   182	 * edge costs reflect terrain difficulty per unit type.
   183	 */
   184	export function makeTerrainCostCallback(
   185	  locomotor: LocomotorInfo,
   186	  getTerrainType: (x: number, y: number) => LandType
   187	): (x: number, y: number) => number {
   188	  return (x: number, y: number): number => {
   189	    const landType = getTerrainType(x, y);
   190	    return locomotor.terrainSpeeds[landType] ?? 0;
   191	  };
   192	}

     1	import type { BlockedByActor } from '../unit/BlockedByActor';
     2	
     3	/**
     4	 * PathNode — 寻路图的基本节点（格子坐标）。
     5	 */
     6	export interface PathNode {
     7	  readonly x: number;
     8	  readonly y: number;
     9	}
    10	
    11	/**
    12	 * 寻路图上下文 — 每次 A* 搜索时传入的动态参数。
    13	 *
    14	 * 不同搜索可能使用不同的阻塞级别（BlockedByActor）、
    15	 * 额外阻塞集合（extraBlocked）或地形代价回调（getTerrainCost）。
    16	 */
    17	export interface PathGraphContext {
    18	  readonly extraBlocked?: ReadonlySet<string>;
    19	  readonly check?: BlockedByActor;
    20	  readonly getTerrainCost?: (x: number, y: number) => number;
    21	  readonly biasSeed?: number;
    22	  /** 父节点坐标 — Task 127 Directed Neighbors 裁剪用 */
    23	  readonly parentNode?: PathNode;
    24	  /** 是否启用 Lane Bias — Task 127 */
    25	  readonly laneBias?: boolean;
    26	  /** Lane Bias 成本偏移量（默认 1）— Task 127 */
    27	  readonly laneBiasCost?: number;
    28	  /** 反向搜索标志 — Task 127 Lane Bias 反向模式 */
    29	  readonly inReverse?: boolean;
    30	}
    31	
    32	/**
    33	 * IPathGraph — 寻路图抽象接口。
    34	 *
    35	 * 将 A* 算法与邻居生成解耦，使 Pathfinder 可以支持多层移动
    36	 * （地面、隧道、地下、跳跃喷气、高架桥等）。
    37	 *
    38	 * OpenRA 对标：
    39	 *   - `OpenRA.Mods.Common/Pathfinder/IPathGraph.cs`
    40	 *   - `OpenRA.Mods.Common/Pathfinder/DensePathGraph.cs`
    41	 */
    42	export interface IPathGraph {
    43	  /**
    44	   * 获取从指定节点出发的所有有效连接。
    45	   * @param node 当前节点
    46	   * @param context 搜索上下文（动态阻塞、地形代价等）
    47	   * @returns 邻居节点及其边代价列表
    48	   */
    49	  getConnections(
    50	    node: PathNode,
    51	    context?: PathGraphContext
    52	  ): ReadonlyArray<{ readonly node: PathNode; readonly cost: number }>;

    56	   * 不同图（地面/空中/地下）可能使用不同的距离度量。
    57	   */

<!-- call_id: tool_NXqsbhpzh8hUILECM5ecS3Ri -->
<system>224 lines read from file starting from line 1. Total lines in file: 224. End of file reached.</system>
     1	import type { IPathGraph, PathGraphContext, PathNode } from './IPathGraph';
     2	import { BlockedByActor } from '../unit/BlockedByActor';
     3	
     4	/**
     5	 * GroundPathGraph — 地面层寻路图。
     6	 *
     7	 * 将 Pathfinder 中原来的邻居生成、阻塞检查、地形代价、
     8	 * 对角线剪枝等逻辑迁移至此，使 Pathfinder 专注于 A* 算法本身。
     9	 *
    10	 * OpenRA 对标：`OpenRA.Mods.Common/Pathfinder/DensePathGraph.cs`
    11	 */
    12	export class GroundPathGraph implements IPathGraph {
    13	  private readonly width: number;
    14	  private readonly height: number;
    15	  private readonly isPassableFn: (x: number, y: number) => boolean;
    16	  private readonly getBlockedCells?: (check?: BlockedByActor) => ReadonlySet<string>;
    17	  private readonly getHeight?: (x: number, y: number) => number;
    18	
    19	  /** 八方向邻居偏移（直线=1，对角线=√2）。 */
    20	  private static readonly NEIGHBORS: ReadonlyArray<{
    21	    readonly x: number;
    22	    readonly y: number;
    23	    readonly cost: number;
    24	  }> = [
    25	    { x: 1, y: 0, cost: 1 },
    26	    { x: -1, y: 0, cost: 1 },
    27	    { x: 0, y: 1, cost: 1 },
    28	    { x: 0, y: -1, cost: 1 },
    29	    { x: 1, y: 1, cost: 1.414 },
    30	    { x: 1, y: -1, cost: 1.414 },
    31	    { x: -1, y: 1, cost: 1.414 },
    32	    { x: -1, y: -1, cost: 1.414 },
    33	  ];
    34	
    35	  /**
    36	   * Directed Neighbors — Task 127
    37	   * 根据父节点方向裁剪邻居集合，避免搜索可从父节点更便宜到达的格子。
    38	   * 索引顺序对应 NEIGHBORS: [E, W, S, N, SE, NE, SW, NW]
    39	   * 映射自 OpenRA DensePathGraph.DirectedNeighbors
    40	   */
    41	  private static readonly DIRECTED_NEIGHBORS: ReadonlyArray<ReadonlyArray<number>> = [
    42	    /* from E  (0) */ [3, 5, 0, 4, 2],
    43	    /* from W  (1) */ [1, 7, 3, 5, 0],
    44	    /* from S  (2) */ [0, 4, 2],
    45	    /* from N  (3) */ [7, 3, 5],
    46	    /* from SE (4) */ [5, 0, 4, 2, 6],
    47	    /* from NE (5) */ [7, 3, 5, 0, 4],
    48	    /* from SW (6) */ [7, 1, 6, 2, 4],
    49	    /* from NW (7) */ [7, 3, 5, 1, 6],
    50	  ];
    51	
    52	  /** Lane Bias 默认成本 */
    53	  private static readonly DEFAULT_LANE_BIAS_COST = 1;
    54	
    55	  constructor(
    56	    width: number,
    57	    height: number,
    58	    isPassable: (x: number, y: number) => boolean,
    59	    getBlockedCells?: (check?: BlockedByActor) => ReadonlySet<string>,
    60	    getHeight?: (x: number, y: number) => number
    61	  ) {
    62	    this.width = width;
    63	    this.height = height;
    64	    this.isPassableFn = isPassable;
    65	    this.getBlockedCells = getBlockedCells;
    66	    this.getHeight = getHeight;
    67	  }
    68	
    69	  getConnections(
    70	    node: PathNode,
    71	    context?: PathGraphContext
    72	  ): ReadonlyArray<{ readonly node: PathNode; readonly cost: number }> {
    73	    const result: Array<{ readonly node: PathNode; readonly cost: number }> = [];
    74	    let neighbors = this.getNeighborsWithBias(context?.biasSeed ?? 0);
    75	    const getTerrainCost = context?.getTerrainCost;
    76	
    77	    // ── Task 127: Directed Neighbors 裁剪 ──
    78	    if (context?.parentNode) {
    79	      const dx = node.x - context.parentNode.x;
    80	      const dy = node.y - context.parentNode.y;
    81	      const dirIdx = this.getNeighborIndex(dx, dy);
    82	      if (dirIdx >= 0) {
    83	        const allowed = new Set(GroundPathGraph.DIRECTED_NEIGHBORS[dirIdx]);
    84	        const filtered: Array<{ readonly x: number; readonly y: number; readonly cost: number }> = [];
    85	        for (let i = 0; i < GroundPathGraph.NEIGHBORS.length; i++) {
    86	          if (allowed.has(i)) {
    87	            filtered.push(GroundPathGraph.NEIGHBORS[i]);
    88	            continue;
    89	          }
    90	          // 被排除的邻居：检查从 parentNode 到该邻居是否实际可达
    91	          // 如果因为地形/阻塞无法从 parentNode 直接到达，则保留
    92	          const off = GroundPathGraph.NEIGHBORS[i];
    93	          const nx = node.x + off.x;
    94	          const ny = node.y + off.y;
    95	          const pdx = nx - context.parentNode.x;
    96	          const pdy = ny - context.parentNode.y;
    97	          if (Math.abs(pdx) > 1 || Math.abs(pdy) > 1) {
    98	            filtered.push(off); // 距离超过 1，parentNode 无法直接到达
    99	            continue;
   100	          }
   101	          // 检查对角线剪枝（如果从 parentNode 到邻居是对角线）
   102	          if (Math.abs(pdx) === 1 && Math.abs(pdy) === 1) {
   103	            const hx = context.parentNode.x + pdx;
   104	            const vy = context.parentNode.y + pdy;
   105	            if (!this.isPassableFn(hx, context.parentNode.y) || !this.isPassableFn(context.parentNode.x, vy)) {
   106	              filtered.push(off);
   107	              continue;
   108	            }
   109	            if (getTerrainCost?.(hx, context.parentNode.y) !== undefined) {
   110	              const t1 = getTerrainCost(hx, context.parentNode.y);
   111	              if (t1 <= 0) {
   112	                filtered.push(off);
   113	                continue;
   114	              }
   115	            }
   116	            if (getTerrainCost?.(context.parentNode.x, vy) !== undefined) {
   117	              const t2 = getTerrainCost(context.parentNode.x, vy);
   118	              if (t2 <= 0) {
   119	                filtered.push(off);
   120	                continue;
   121	              }
   122	            }
   123	          }
   124	          // 可以从 parentNode 直接到达，排除（节省搜索节点）
   125	        }
   126	        neighbors = filtered;
   127	      }
   128	    }
   129	
   130	    const dynamicBlocked = this.getBlockedCells?.(context?.check ?? BlockedByActor.All) ?? new Set<string>();
   131	    const extraBlocked = context?.extraBlocked;
   132	    const laneBias = context?.laneBias ?? false;
   133	    const laneBiasCost = context?.laneBiasCost ?? GroundPathGraph.DEFAULT_LANE_BIAS_COST;
   134	    const inReverse = context?.inReverse ?? false;
   135	
   136	    for (const offset of neighbors) {
   137	      const nx = node.x + offset.x;
   138	      const ny = node.y + offset.y;
   139	
   140	      if (!this.isInside({ x: nx, y: ny })) continue;
   141	      if (!this.isPassableFn(nx, ny)) continue;
   142	
   143	      // ── Task 130: Height discontinuity check ──
   144	      if (this.getHeight) {
   145	        const hSrc = this.getHeight(node.x, node.y);
   146	        const hDst = this.getHeight(nx, ny);
   147	        if (Math.abs(hSrc - hDst) > 1) continue; // Cliff — impassable
   148	      }
   149	
   150	      const key = `${nx},${ny}`;
   151	      if (dynamicBlocked.has(key)) continue;
   152	      if (extraBlocked?.has(key)) continue;
   153	
   154	      // ── 对角线剪枝（Corner Cutting）──
   155	      if (Math.abs(offset.x) === 1 && Math.abs(offset.y) === 1) {
   156	        const hx = node.x + offset.x;
   157	        const vy = node.y + offset.y;
   158	        if (!this.isPassableFn(hx, node.y)) continue;
   159	        if (!this.isPassableFn(node.x, vy)) continue;
   160	        if (dynamicBlocked.has(`${hx},${node.y}`) || extraBlocked?.has(`${hx},${node.y}`)) continue;
   161	        if (dynamicBlocked.has(`${node.x},${vy}`) || extraBlocked?.has(`${node.x},${vy}`)) continue;
   162	        if (getTerrainCost && getTerrainCost(hx, node.y) <= 0) continue;
   163	        if (getTerrainCost && getTerrainCost(node.x, vy) <= 0) continue;
   164	      }
   165	
   166	      // ── 地形代价 ──
   167	      const terrainCost = getTerrainCost?.(nx, ny) ?? 1;
   168	      if (terrainCost <= 0) continue;
   169	
   170	      let cost = offset.cost / terrainCost;
   171	
   172	      // ── Task 127: Lane Bias ──
   173	      if (laneBias) {
   174	        const ux = (nx + (inReverse ? 1 : 0)) & 1;
   175	        const uy = (ny + (inReverse ? 1 : 0)) & 1;
   176	        if ((ux === 0 && offset.y < 0) || (ux === 1 && offset.y > 0)) cost += laneBiasCost;
   177	        if ((uy === 0 && offset.x < 0) || (uy === 1 && offset.x > 0)) cost += laneBiasCost;
   178	      }
   179	
   180	      result.push({ node: { x: nx, y: ny }, cost });
   181	    }
   182	
   183	    return result;
   184	  }
   185	
   186	  /** 根据偏移量查找在 NEIGHBORS 中的索引，用于 Directed Neighbors */
   187	  private getNeighborIndex(dx: number, dy: number): number {
   188	    for (let i = 0; i < GroundPathGraph.NEIGHBORS.length; i++) {
   189	      if (GroundPathGraph.NEIGHBORS[i].x === dx && GroundPathGraph.NEIGHBORS[i].y === dy) return i;
   190	    }
   191	    return -1;
   192	  }
   193	
   194	  getHeuristic(a: PathNode, b: PathNode): number {
   195	    const dx = Math.abs(a.x - b.x);
   196	    const dy = Math.abs(a.y - b.y);
   197	    return Math.max(dx, dy) + (Math.sqrt(2) - 1) * Math.min(dx, dy);
   198	  }
   199	
   200	  isInside(node: PathNode): boolean {
   201	    return node.x >= 0 && node.x < this.width && node.y >= 0 && node.y < this.height;
   202	  }
   203	
   204	  isPassable(node: PathNode): boolean {
   205	    return this.isInside(node) && this.isPassableFn(node.x, node.y);
   206	  }
   207	
   208	  /** 基于 biasSeed 对邻居遍历顺序做 Fisher-Yates 洗牌。 */
   209	  private getNeighborsWithBias(seed: number): ReadonlyArray<{
   210	    readonly x: number;
   211	    readonly y: number;
   212	    readonly cost: number;
   213	  }> {
   214	    if (seed === 0) return GroundPathGraph.NEIGHBORS;
   215	    const dirs = [...GroundPathGraph.NEIGHBORS];
   216	    let s = Math.abs(seed);
   217	    for (let i = dirs.length - 1; i > 0; i--) {
   218	      s = (s * 16807) % 2147483647;
   219	      const j = s % (i + 1);
   220	      [dirs[i], dirs[j]] = [dirs[j], dirs[i]];
   221	    }
   222	    return dirs;
   223	  }
   224	}


</details>

     9	/**
    10	 * A* 寻路 — 基于 IPathGraph 抽象的多层寻路器。
    11	 *
    12	 * Task 23.19 重构：将邻居生成逻辑迁移到 GroundPathGraph，

    64	    isPassable: (x: number, y: number) => boolean,
    65	    getBlockedCells?: (check?: BlockedByActor) => ReadonlySet<string>,
    66	    getTerrainType?: (x: number, y: number) => LandType,
    67	    getHeight?: (x: number, y: number) => number
    68	  ) {
    69	    this.width = width;
    70	    this.height = height;
    71	    this.isPassable = isPassable;
    72	    this.getBlockedCells = getBlockedCells;
    73	    this.getTerrainType = getTerrainType;
    74	    this.getHeight = getHeight;
    75	    this.hierarchical = new HierarchicalPathfinder(width, height, isPassable);
    76	    this.groundGraph = new GroundPathGraph(width, height, isPassable, getBlockedCells, getHeight);
    77	    this.cellInfoPool = new CellInfoLayerPool(width, height, 4);
    78	  }
    79	
    80	  /**
    81	   * A* 寻路（八方向）。
    82	   * @param extraBlocked 可选的额外阻塞格子集合（格式 `"x,y"`），用于单位间动态避障。
    83	   * @param getTerrainCost 可选的地形代价回调，返回该格子的速度倍率（0 = 不可通行）。
    84	   *                       当提供时，A* 边代价 = `distance / terrainCost`。
    85	   * @returns 从起点到终点的格子路径（含起点和终点），无路径时返回 `null`。
    86	   */
    87	  findPath(
    88	    startX: number,
    89	    startY: number,
    90	    endX: number,
    91	    endY: number,
    92	    extraBlocked?: ReadonlySet<string>,
    93	    check = BlockedByActor.All,
    94	    biasSeed = 0,
    95	    allowBlockedEnd = false,
    96	    getTerrainCost?: (x: number, y: number) => number,
    97	    /** Task 132: 启发式权重（1.0 = 严格可采纳，1.25 = OpenRA 默认） */
    98	    heuristicWeight = 1.0,
    99	    /** Task 127: 是否启用 Lane Bias */
   100	    laneBias = false,
   101	    /** Task 127: Lane Bias 成本 */
   102	    laneBiasCost = 1
   103	  ): PathNode[] | null {
   104	    if (!this.isInside(endX, endY) || !this.isPassable(endX, endY)) return null;
   105	
   106	    // ── Task 23.13: Hierarchical quick reject ──
   107	    if (!this.hierarchical.areConnected(startX, startY, endX, endY)) return null;
   108	
   109	    const dynamicBlocked = this.getBlockedCells?.(check) ?? new Set<string>();
   110	    if (!allowBlockedEnd && (dynamicBlocked.has(`${endX},${endY}`) || extraBlocked?.has(`${endX},${endY}`)))
   111	      return null;
   112	
   113	    const openSet = new BinaryHeap<AStarNode>((a, b) => a - b, nodeKey);
   114	    const closedSet = new Set<string>();
   115	
   116	    const startNode: AStarNode = {
   117	      x: startX,
   118	      y: startY,
   119	      g: 0,
   120	      h: this.groundGraph.getHeuristic({ x: startX, y: startY }, { x: endX, y: endY }),
   121	      f: 0,
   122	      parent: null,
   123	    };
   124	    startNode.f = startNode.g + startNode.h * heuristicWeight;
   125	    openSet.push(startNode, startNode.f);
   126	
   127	    const graphContext: PathGraphContext = {
   128	      getTerrainCost,
   129	      biasSeed,
   130	      laneBias,
   131	      laneBiasCost,
   132	    };
   133	
   134	    while (!openSet.isEmpty()) {
   135	      const current = openSet.pop()!;
   136	
   137	      if (current.x === endX && current.y === endY) {
   138	        return this.reconstructPath(current);
   139	      }
   140	
   141	      closedSet.add(`${current.x},${current.y}`);
   142	
   143	      // Task 127: 传递父节点用于 Directed Neighbors
   144	      const connContext: PathGraphContext = {
   145	        ...graphContext,
   146	        parentNode: current.parent ? { x: current.parent.x, y: current.parent.y } : undefined,
   147	      };
   148	
   149	      const connections = this.groundGraph.getConnections({ x: current.x, y: current.y }, connContext);
   150	      for (const conn of connections) {
   151	        const nx = conn.node.x;
   152	        const ny = conn.node.y;
   153	        const key = `${nx},${ny}`;
   154	
   155	        if (closedSet.has(key)) continue;
   156	
   157	        // ── 动态阻塞检查（搜索级别，GroundPathGraph 不过滤阻塞）──
   158	        const isEndCell = nx === endX && ny === endY;
   159	        if (!isEndCell && (dynamicBlocked.has(key) || extraBlocked?.has(key))) continue;
   160	        if (!allowBlockedEnd && isEndCell && (dynamicBlocked.has(key) || extraBlocked?.has(key))) continue;
   161	
   162	        const g = current.g + conn.cost;
   163	        const existing = openSet.has({ x: nx, y: ny, g: 0, h: 0, f: 0, parent: null });
   164	
   165	        if (!existing) {
   166	          const h = this.groundGraph.getHeuristic({ x: nx, y: ny }, { x: endX, y: endY });
   167	          const node: AStarNode = { x: nx, y: ny, g, h, f: g + h * heuristicWeight, parent: current };
   168	          openSet.push(node, node.f);
   169	        } else {
   170	          // key 已存在：BinaryHeap.push 会自动 decrease-key（若新 f 更小）
   171	          const h = this.groundGraph.getHeuristic({ x: nx, y: ny }, { x: endX, y: endY });
   172	          const node: AStarNode = { x: nx, y: ny, g, h, f: g + h * heuristicWeight, parent: current };
   173	          openSet.push(node, node.f);
   174	        }
   175	      }
   176	    }
   177	
   178	    return null;
   179	  }
   180	
   181	  private isInside(x: number, y: number): boolean {
   182	    return x >= 0 && x < this.width && y >= 0 && y < this.height;
   183	  }
   184	
   185	  /** 检查指定格子是否在地图范围内且地形可通行。 */
   186	  isCellPassable(x: number, y: number): boolean {
   187	    return this.groundGraph.isPassable({ x, y });
   188	  }
   189	
   190	  // ── Task 23.14: Bidirectional A* ──
   191	
   192	  findPathBidirectional(
   193	    startX: number,
   194	    startY: number,
   195	    endX: number,
   196	    endY: number,
   197	    extraBlocked?: ReadonlySet<string>,
   198	    check = BlockedByActor.All,
   199	    biasSeed = 0,
   200	    allowBlockedEnd = false,
   201	    getTerrainCost?: (x: number, y: number) => number,
   202	    /** Task 132: 启发式权重 */
   203	    heuristicWeight = 1.0,
   204	    /** Task 127: Lane Bias */
   205	    laneBias = false,
   206	    laneBiasCost = 1
   207	  ): PathNode[] | null {
   208	    if (!this.isInside(endX, endY) || !this.isPassable(endX, endY)) return null;
   209	    if (!this.hierarchical.areConnected(startX, startY, endX, endY)) return null;
   210	
   211	    const dynamicBlocked = this.getBlockedCells?.(check) ?? new Set<string>();
   212	    if (!allowBlockedEnd && (dynamicBlocked.has(`${endX},${endY}`) || extraBlocked?.has(`${endX},${endY}`)))
   213	      return null;
   214	
   215	    const forwardOpen = new BinaryHeap<AStarNode>((a, b) => a - b, nodeKey);
   216	    const forwardClosed = new Set<string>();
   217	    const forwardG = new Map<string, number>();
   218	    const forwardParent = new Map<string, AStarNode>();
   219	
   220	    const backwardOpen = new BinaryHeap<AStarNode>((a, b) => a - b, nodeKey);
   221	    const backwardClosed = new Set<string>();
   222	    const backwardG = new Map<string, number>();
   223	    const backwardParent = new Map<string, AStarNode>();
   224	
   225	    const startNode: AStarNode = {
   226	      x: startX,
   227	      y: startY,
   228	      g: 0,
   229	      h: this.groundGraph.getHeuristic({ x: startX, y: startY }, { x: endX, y: endY }),
   230	      f: 0,
   231	      parent: null,
   232	    };
   233	    startNode.f = startNode.g + startNode.h * heuristicWeight;
   234	    forwardOpen.push(startNode, startNode.f);
   235	    forwardG.set(`${startX},${startY}`, 0);
   236	
   237	    const endNode: AStarNode = {
   238	      x: endX,
   239	      y: endY,
   240	      g: 0,
   241	      h: this.groundGraph.getHeuristic({ x: endX, y: endY }, { x: startX, y: startY }),
   242	      f: 0,
   243	      parent: null,
   244	    };
   245	    endNode.f = endNode.g + endNode.h * heuristicWeight;
   246	    backwardOpen.push(endNode, endNode.f);
   247	    backwardG.set(`${endX},${endY}`, 0);
   248	
   249	    let bestMeeting: { node: AStarNode; totalG: number } | null = null;
   250	
   251	    const graphContext: PathGraphContext = {
   252	      getTerrainCost,
   253	      biasSeed,
   254	      laneBias,
   255	      laneBiasCost,
   256	    };
   257	
   258	    while (!forwardOpen.isEmpty() && !backwardOpen.isEmpty()) {
   259	      const forwardF = forwardOpen.peekPriority() ?? Infinity;
   260	      const backwardF = backwardOpen.peekPriority() ?? Infinity;
   261	      const useForward = forwardF <= backwardF;
   262	
   263	      const current = useForward ? forwardOpen.pop()! : backwardOpen.pop()!;
   264	      const key = `${current.x},${current.y}`;
   265	
   266	      if (useForward) {
   267	        if (forwardClosed.has(key)) continue;
   268	        forwardClosed.add(key);
   269	        if (backwardClosed.has(key) || backwardG.has(key)) {
   270	          const bg = backwardG.get(key) ?? Infinity;
   271	          const total = (forwardG.get(key) ?? Infinity) + bg;
   272	          if (!bestMeeting || total < bestMeeting.totalG) {
   273	            bestMeeting = { node: current, totalG: total };
   274	          }
   275	        }
   276	      } else {
   277	        if (backwardClosed.has(key)) continue;
   278	        backwardClosed.add(key);
   279	        if (forwardClosed.has(key) || forwardG.has(key)) {
   280	          const fg = forwardG.get(key) ?? Infinity;
   281	          const total = fg + (backwardG.get(key) ?? Infinity);
   282	          if (!bestMeeting || total < bestMeeting.totalG) {
   283	            bestMeeting = { node: current, totalG: total };
   284	          }
   285	        }
   286	      }
   287	
   288	      const minF = Math.min(forwardOpen.peekPriority() ?? Infinity, backwardOpen.peekPriority() ?? Infinity);
   289	      if (bestMeeting && minF >= bestMeeting.totalG) {
   290	        break;
   291	      }
   292	
   293	      // Task 127: 传递父节点 + inReverse 标志
   294	      const connContext: PathGraphContext = {
   295	        ...graphContext,
   296	        parentNode: current.parent ? { x: current.parent.x, y: current.parent.y } : undefined,
   297	        inReverse: !useForward,
   298	      };
   299	
   300	      const connections = this.groundGraph.getConnections({ x: current.x, y: current.y }, connContext);
   301	      for (const conn of connections) {
   302	        const nx = conn.node.x;
   303	        const ny = conn.node.y;
   304	        const nKey = `${nx},${ny}`;
   305	
   306	        if (!this.isInside(nx, ny)) continue;
   307	        if (!this.isPassable(nx, ny)) continue;
   308	
   309	        const isEndCell = nx === endX && ny === endY;
   310	        if (!isEndCell && (dynamicBlocked.has(nKey) || extraBlocked?.has(nKey))) continue;
   311	        if (!allowBlockedEnd && isEndCell && (dynamicBlocked.has(nKey) || extraBlocked?.has(nKey))) continue;
   312	
   313	        const g = current.g + conn.cost;
   314	        const gMap = useForward ? forwardG : backwardG;
   315	        const parentMap = useForward ? forwardParent : backwardParent;
   316	        const existingG = gMap.get(nKey);
   317	
   318	        if (existingG === undefined || g < existingG) {
   319	          gMap.set(nKey, g);
   320	          parentMap.set(nKey, current);
   321	          const h = useForward
   322	            ? this.groundGraph.getHeuristic({ x: nx, y: ny }, { x: endX, y: endY })
   323	            : this.groundGraph.getHeuristic({ x: nx, y: ny }, { x: startX, y: startY });
   324	          const node: AStarNode = { x: nx, y: ny, g, h, f: g + h * heuristicWeight, parent: null };
   325	          const open = useForward ? forwardOpen : backwardOpen;
   326	          open.push(node, node.f);
   327	        }
   328	      }
   329	    }
   330	
   331	    if (!bestMeeting) return null;
   332	
   333	    const forwardPart = this.reconstructPathBidirectional(bestMeeting.node, forwardParent, startX, startY);
   334	    const backwardPart = this.reconstructPathBidirectional(bestMeeting.node, backwardParent, endX, endY);
   335	    backwardPart.shift();
   336	    return [...forwardPart, ...backwardPart];
   337	  }
   338	
   339	  /**
   340	   * Predicate Search — 搜索到第一个满足条件的格子即停止。
   341	   * 用于 MoveWithinRange（找环形范围内的可达格子）等场景。
   342	   */
   343	  findPathToPredicate(
   344	    startX: number,
   345	    startY: number,
   346	    predicate: (x: number, y: number) => boolean,
   347	    maxDistance = Infinity,
   348	    extraBlocked?: ReadonlySet<string>,
   349	    check = BlockedByActor.All,
   350	    biasSeed = 0,
   351	    getTerrainCost?: (x: number, y: number) => number,
   352	    /** Task 132: 启发式权重（Predicate 搜索通常不需要，为接口一致性保留） */
   353	    heuristicWeight = 1.0,
   354	    /** Task 127: Lane Bias */
   355	    laneBias = false,
   356	    laneBiasCost = 1
   357	  ): PathNode[] | null {
   358	    const dynamicBlocked = this.getBlockedCells?.(check) ?? new Set<string>();
   359	
   360	    const openSet = new BinaryHeap<AStarNode>((a, b) => a - b, nodeKey);
   361	    const closedSet = new Set<string>();
   362	
   363	    const startNode: AStarNode = {
   364	      x: startX,
   365	      y: startY,
   366	      g: 0,
   367	      h: 0,
   368	      f: 0,
   369	      parent: null,
   370	    };
   371	    openSet.push(startNode, 0);
   372	
   373	    const graphContext: PathGraphContext = {
   374	      getTerrainCost,
   375	      biasSeed,
   376	      laneBias,
   377	      laneBiasCost,
   378	    };
   379	
   380	    while (!openSet.isEmpty()) {
   381	      const current = openSet.pop()!;
   382	
   383	      if (predicate(current.x, current.y)) {
   384	        return this.reconstructPath(current);
   385	      }
   386	
   387	      closedSet.add(`${current.x},${current.y}`);
   388	
   389	      if (current.g >= maxDistance) continue;
   390	
   391	      // Task 127: 传递父节点
   392	      const connContext: PathGraphContext = {
   393	        ...graphContext,
   394	        parentNode: current.parent ? { x: current.parent.x, y: current.parent.y } : undefined,
   395	      };
   396	
   397	      const connections = this.groundGraph.getConnections({ x: current.x, y: current.y }, connContext);
   398	      for (const conn of connections) {
   399	        const nx = conn.node.x;
   400	        const ny = conn.node.y;
   401	        const key = `${nx},${ny}`;
   402	
   403	        if (closedSet.has(key)) continue;
   404	        if (dynamicBlocked.has(key) || extraBlocked?.has(key)) continue;
   405	
   406	        const g = current.g + conn.cost;
   407	        const existing = openSet.has({ x: nx, y: ny, g: 0, h: 0, f: 0, parent: null });
   408	
   409	        if (!existing) {
   410	          const node: AStarNode = { x: nx, y: ny, g, h: 0, f: g * heuristicWeight, parent: current };
   411	          openSet.push(node, node.f);
   412	        } else {
   413	          const node: AStarNode = { x: nx, y: ny, g, h: 0, f: g * heuristicWeight, parent: current };
   414	          openSet.push(node, node.f);
   415	        }
   416	      }
   417	    }
   418	
   419	    return null;
   420	  }
   421	
   422	  // ── Helpers ──
   423	
   424	  private reconstructPathBidirectional(
   425	    meetingNode: AStarNode,
   426	    parentMap: Map<string, AStarNode>,
   427	    startX: number,
   428	    startY: number
   429	  ): PathNode[] {
   430	    const path: PathNode[] = [{ x: meetingNode.x, y: meetingNode.y }];
   431	    let key = `${meetingNode.x},${meetingNode.y}`;
   432	    const visited = new Set<string>([key]);
   433	
   434	    while (parentMap.has(key)) {
   435	      const parent = parentMap.get(key)!;
   436	      key = `${parent.x},${parent.y}`;
   437	      if (visited.has(key)) break;
   438	      visited.add(key);
   439	      path.unshift({ x: parent.x, y: parent.y });
   440	      if (parent.x === startX && parent.y === startY) break;
   441	    }
   442	    return path;
   443	  }
   444	
   445	  private reconstructPath(endNode: AStarNode): PathNode[] {
   446	    const path: PathNode[] = [];
   447	    let current: AStarNode | null = endNode;
   448	    while (current) {
   449	      path.unshift({ x: current.x, y: current.y });
   450	      current = current.parent;
   451	    }
   452	    return path;
   453	  }
   454	}


</details>

<!-- call_id: tool_Gt5XRYWs1Zqt2oINbULfAQEu -->

    51	  /** 根据 unitId 生成确定性等待偏移，防止多单位同步死锁。 */
    52	  private getWaitOffset(unitId: string): number {
    53	    const code = unitId.charCodeAt(unitId.length - 1);
    54	    return (code % 3) * (this.locomotor.waitSpread / 2);
    55	  }
    56	
    57	  /** 根据 unitId 生成 A* 方向偏好种子，让不同单位绕路时分流。 */
    58	  private getBiasSeed(unitId: string): number {
    59	    let hash = 0;
    60	    for (let i = 0; i < unitId.length; i++) {
    61	      hash = (hash * 31 + unitId.charCodeAt(i)) % 1000000007;
    62	    }
    63	    return hash;
    64	  }

<details><summary>Thinking</summary>

现在我对现有代码有了清晰的了解。当前没有海军单位定义，没有 WaterPathGraph，也没有 ShipTrait。

Task-VEH2 需要：
1. `WaterPathGraph` — 仅水格可通行的寻路图
2. `ShipTrait` — 海军单位行为，转向慢、惯性大
3. 船坞建筑、登陆艇

让我制定计划：

### 1. WaterPathGraph
- 类似于 `GroundPathGraph`，但 `isPassableFn` 只返回水格（Water/Beach/River）可通行
- 不需要 Height check（水面没有悬崖）
- 仍然需要 Directed Neighbors、Lane Bias 等优化

### 2. ShipTrait
- 扩展 Trait 基类
- 属性：turnSpeed（很低，比如 30-45 deg/s）、inertia（惯性系数）
- 状态：Idle, Moving, Turning
- 移动时带有惯性（速度不会立即变化）
- 必须在水面上移动

### 3. 海军单位定义
- 在 `UnitDefinitions.ts` 中添加：
  - `Gunboat` — 轻型快速舰船
  - `Destroyer` — 重型舰船
  - `Submarine` — 潜艇
  - `Transport` — 运输船/登陆艇

### 4. Pathfinder 扩展
- 支持 `waterGraph`，或者创建独立的 `NavalPathfinder`

实际上，从设计角度看，最简洁的方式是：
- `WaterPathGraph` 继承或复制 `GroundPathGraph` 的接口
- `Pathfinder` 新增 `waterGraph` 属性
- `ShipTrait` 是一个新的 Trait，可以与现有的 `Mobile` 系统配合

但等一下，查看现有的 `UnitMovement.ts`，它使用的是 `Unit` 类（旧架构）而不是 Actor/Trait 架构。新任务应该基于 Actor/Trait 架构。

让我检查一下新的 Actor/Trait 架构下移动是如何实现的。

</details>

<details><summary>Thinking</summary>

Actor/Trait 架构下已有：
- `ArmamentTrait`
- `ConditionalTrait` / `UpgradeableTrait`
- `GrantConditionOnPrerequisite`
- `HealthTrait`
- `RenderTrait`
- `AircraftTrait`
- `Reservable`

但没有 `MobileTrait` 或地面移动 Trait。这意味着 Actor/Trait 架构下的移动系统可能还在旧架构中。

Task-VEH2 需要在 Actor/Trait 架构下实现海军。由于 TODO 要求的是基础功能，我应该：
1. 创建 `WaterPathGraph` — 水面寻路图
2. 创建 `ShipTrait` — 海军单位 Trait（基于 Actor/Trait）
3. 在 `UnitDefinitions.ts` 中添加海军单位定义
4. 写 e2e 测试

让我先查看 `AircraftTrait.ts` 看看 Trait 的完整实现模式。

</details>

    10	import { Trait } from '../traits/Trait';
    11	
    12	export interface AircraftTraitOptions {
    13	  /** 巡航高度（世界单位）。 */
    14	  cruiseAltitude: number;
    15	  /** 着陆高度（世界单位）。 */
    16	  landAltitude: number;
    17	  /** 是否可悬停（直升机）。 */
    18	  canHover: boolean;
    19	  /** 飞行速度（世界单位/秒）。 */
    20	  speed: number;
    21	  /** 转弯半径（世界单位）。 */
    22	  turnRadius: number;
    23	}
    24	
    25	/** Aircraft 状态机。 */
    26	export enum AircraftState {
    27	  Idle = 'Idle',
    28	  TakeOff = 'TakeOff',
    29	  Cruise = 'Cruise',
    30	  Landing = 'Landing',
    31	  Hover = 'Hover',
    32	  Docked = 'Docked',
    33	}
    34	
    35	/**
    36	 * AircraftTrait — 挂载到 Actor 上，管理空中单位的飞行状态。
    37	 */
    38	export class AircraftTrait extends Trait {
    39	  private options: AircraftTraitOptions;
    40	  private state = AircraftState.Idle;
    41	  private altitude = 0;
    42	  private targetX = 0;
    43	  private targetY = 0;
    44	  private facing = 0;
    45	
    46	  constructor(options: AircraftTraitOptions) {
    47	    super();
    48	    this.options = options;
    49	    this.altitude = options.landAltitude;
    50	  }
    51	
    52	  getState(): AircraftState {
    53	    return this.state;
    54	  }
    55	
    56	  getAltitude(): number {
    57	    return this.altitude;
    58	  }
    59	
    60	  getFacing(): number {
    61	    return this.facing;
    62	  }
    63	
    64	  /** 命令飞机起飞并飞往目标。 */
    65	  flyTo(_actor: Actor, x: number, y: number): void {
    66	    if (this.state === AircraftState.Docked) {
    67	      this.state = AircraftState.TakeOff;
    68	    } else {
    69	      this.state = AircraftState.Cruise;
    70	    }
    71	    this.targetX = x;
    72	    this.targetY = y;
    73	  }
    74	
    75	  /** 命令飞机返回并着陆。 */
    76	  land(_actor: Actor): void {
    77	    this.state = AircraftState.Landing;
    78	  }
    79	
    80	  /** 命令飞机悬停（仅 canHover=true）。 */
    81	  hover(_actor: Actor): void {
    82	    if (this.options.canHover) {
    83	      this.state = AircraftState.Hover;
    84	    }
    85	  }
    86	
    87	  override tick(actor: Actor, deltaTime: number): void {
    88	    const dt = deltaTime / 1000; // ms → s
    89	
    90	    switch (this.state) {
    91	      case AircraftState.TakeOff: {
    92	        // 爬升到巡航高度
    93	        this.altitude += this.options.speed * dt * 0.5;
    94	        if (this.altitude >= this.options.cruiseAltitude) {
    95	          this.altitude = this.options.cruiseAltitude;
    96	          this.state = AircraftState.Cruise;
    97	        }
    98	        break;
    99	      }
   100	      case AircraftState.Cruise: {
   101	        this.altitude = this.options.cruiseAltitude;
   102	        this.moveTowardsTarget(actor, dt);
   103	        break;
   104	      }
   105	      case AircraftState.Landing: {
   106	        // 下降并移动到着陆点
   107	        this.moveTowardsTarget(actor, dt);
   108	        this.altitude -= this.options.speed * dt * 0.3;
   109	        if (this.altitude <= this.options.landAltitude) {
   110	          this.altitude = this.options.landAltitude;
   111	          this.state = AircraftState.Docked;
   112	        }
   113	        break;
   114	      }
   115	      case AircraftState.Hover: {
   116	        this.altitude = this.options.cruiseAltitude;
   117	        break;
   118	      }
   119	      case AircraftState.Idle:
   120	      case AircraftState.Docked:
   121	        break;
   122	    }
   123	
   124	    // 同步 Actor 的世界坐标（Z = 高度）
   125	    actor.x = this.targetX;
   126	    actor.y = this.targetY;
   127	  }
   128	
   129	  private moveTowardsTarget(_actor: Actor, _dt: number): void {
   130	    // 简化的方向更新
   131	    const dx = this.targetX - _actor.x;
   132	    const dy = this.targetY - _actor.y;
   133	    const dist = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
   134	    if (dist > 0.1) {
   135	      this.facing = Math.atan2(dy, dx);
   136	      // 只更新 facing，不实际移动 Actor（由路径系统处理）
   137	    }
   138	  }
   139	}
   140	
   141	/**
   142	 * Reservable — 机场/停机坪的停机位 Trait。
   143	 * 管理有限的停机位槽位，供 Aircraft 降落占用。
   144	 */
   145	export class Reservable extends Trait {
   146	  private maxSlots: number;
   147	  private occupiedSlots = 0;
   148	  private reservations = new Map<string, { x: number; y: number }>();
   149	
   150	  constructor(maxSlots: number) {
   151	    super();
   152	    this.maxSlots = maxSlots;
   153	  }
   154	
   155	  /** 尝试预留一个停机位。 */
   156	  reserve(id: string, x: number, y: number): boolean {
   157	    if (this.occupiedSlots >= this.maxSlots) return false;
   158	    if (this.reservations.has(id)) return true;
   159	    this.reservations.set(id, { x, y });
   160	    this.occupiedSlots++;
   161	    return true;
   162	  }
   163	
   164	  /** 释放停机位。 */
   165	  release(id: string): boolean {
   166	    if (!this.reservations.has(id)) return false;
   167	    this.reservations.delete(id);
   168	    this.occupiedSlots--;
   169	    return true;
   170	  }
   171	
   172	  /** 获取指定预留的着陆坐标。 */
   173	  getReservation(id: string): { x: number; y: number } | undefined {
   174	    return this.reservations.get(id);
   175	  }
   176	
   177	  getOccupiedCount(): number {
   178	    return this.occupiedSlots;
   179	  }
   180	
   181	  getMaxSlots(): number {
   182	    return this.maxSlots;
   183	  }
   184	
   185	  hasReservation(id: string): boolean {
   186	    return this.reservations.has(id);
   187	  }
   188	}


</details>

<details><summary>Thinking</summary>

让我创建 WaterPathGraph.ts。它应该与 GroundPathGraph 结构类似，但只在水格上通行。

实际上，我注意到 `GroundPathGraph` 的 `isPassableFn` 是一个外部传入的函数，所以理论上可以用同一个 `GroundPathGraph` 类，只是传入不同的 `isPassable` 函数。但 TODO 明确要求创建 `WaterPathGraph`，所以我还是创建一个新类。

不过更好的设计是：`WaterPathGraph` 可以继承 `GroundPathGraph`，或者复用其代码。但 `GroundPathGraph` 不是 abstract 的，且有 Height check 等逻辑对水面不适用。

最简洁的方式：让 `WaterPathGraph` 独立实现 `IPathGraph`，复用 `GroundPathGraph` 的核心逻辑但去掉 Height check。

实际上，再想想：`GroundPathGraph` 已经通过构造函数参数非常灵活了。`isPassableFn` 可以传入只返回水格可通行的函数，`getHeight` 可以传 `undefined`。所以 `WaterPathGraph` 可以是一个 thin wrapper，或者直接让 `Pathfinder` 支持 `waterGraph`。

但 TODO 明确要求 `WaterPathGraph`，所以我创建它。让我做一个简洁的实现：直接实例化 `GroundPathGraph` 但传入水面专用的 `isPassable`。这样代码复用最好。

不，等等。`GroundPathGraph` 的 `getConnections` 中有 Height check：
```typescript
if (this.getHeight) {
  const hSrc = this.getHeight(node.x, node.y);
  const hDst = this.getHeight(nx, ny);
  if (Math.abs(hSrc - hDst) > 1) continue;
}
```

如果 `getHeight` 不传，就不会执行。所以 `WaterPathGraph` 完全可以复用 `GroundPathGraph` 的代码。

我的方案：
1. `WaterPathGraph` 是一个工厂函数或包装类，创建配置了水面 `isPassable` 的 `GroundPathGraph`
2. 或者更直接：`Pathfinder` 中新增 `waterGraph`，使用与 `groundGraph` 相同的 `GroundPathGraph` 类，但 `isPassable` 函数不同

等等，让我重新思考。TODO 说的是：
- `WaterPathGraph`：仅水格可通行
- `Ship` Trait：转向慢、惯性大

`WaterPathGraph` 应该是一个独立的类，因为未来可能有不同的启发函数（水面移动可能不考虑对角线捷径等）。但最简单的做法是直接复用 `GroundPathGraph`。

我决定：
1. `WaterPathGraph` 是一个类，内部使用 `GroundPathGraph`，但 `isPassable` 只返回水格
2. 或者更简单：直接暴露一个 `createWaterPathGraph` 函数

不，最符合 TODO 期望的方式是创建 `WaterPathGraph` 类，实现 `IPathGraph`：

```typescript
export class WaterPathGraph implements IPathGraph {
  private graph: GroundPathGraph;
  
  constructor(width, height, getTerrainType) {
    const isWaterPassable = (x, y) => {
      const t = getTerrainType(x, y);
      return t === LandType.Water || t === LandType.Beach || t === LandType.River;
    };
    this.graph = new GroundPathGraph(width, height, isWaterPassable);
  }
  
  getConnections(...) { return this.graph.getConnections(...); }
  getHeuristic(...) { return this.graph.getHeuristic(...); }
  isInside(...) { return this.graph.isInside(...); }
  isPassable(...) { return this.graph.isPassable(...); }
}
```

这样就简洁地复用了 `GroundPathGraph` 的所有优化逻辑。

然后 `Pathfinder` 需要支持 `waterGraph`。

<details><summary>Thinking</summary>

现在创建 ShipTrait.ts。ShipTrait 需要：
- 转向慢（turnSpeed 很低，比如 45 deg/s）
- 惯性大（速度不会立即达到最大值）
- 基于 Actor/Trait 架构
- 状态机：Idle, Moving, Turning
- 需要寻路系统支持

让我设计 ShipTrait：

```typescript
export interface ShipTraitOptions {
  speed: number;        // 最大速度（世界单位/秒）
  turnSpeed: number;    // 转向速度（度/秒）
  inertia: number;      // 惯性系数 0-1，越高加速越慢
}

export enum ShipState {
  Idle = 'Idle',
  Moving = 'Moving',
  Turning = 'Turning',
}

export class ShipTrait extends Trait {
  private options: ShipTraitOptions;
  private state = ShipState.Idle;
  private currentSpeed = 0;
  private facing = 0;      // 当前朝向（弧度）
  private targetFacing = 0; // 目标朝向
  private targetX = 0;
  private targetY = 0;
  
  // tick 中：
  // 1. 如果 state == Moving，先计算目标朝向
  // 2. 如果当前朝向与目标朝向差距大，切换到 Turning
  // 3. Turning 时按 turnSpeed 逐步转向
  // 4. 转向完成后切换到 Moving，按惯性加速到目标速度
  // 5. 移动位置
}
```

等等， Ship 的移动应该基于路径点（PathNode[]）。但 AircraftTrait 目前没有路径系统，它直接飞往目标。Ship 应该类似，沿着路径移动。

但 Ship 的关键特性是：
1. 转向慢 — 必须缓慢转向目标方向
2. 惯性大 — 速度不会突变

让我写一个简洁但体现这些特性的实现：

```typescript
export class ShipTrait extends Trait {
  // ...
  override tick(actor: Actor, deltaTime: number): void {
    const dt = deltaTime / 1000;
    
    if (this.state === ShipState.Idle) return;
    
    // 计算到目标的方向
    const dx = this.targetX - actor.x;
    const dy = this.targetY - actor.y;
    const dist = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
    
    if (dist < 0.1) {
      this.currentSpeed = 0;
      this.state = ShipState.Idle;
      return;
    }
    
    this.targetFacing = Math.atan2(dy, dx);
    
    // 转向
    const angleDiff = this.normalizeAngle(this.targetFacing - this.facing);
    const maxTurn = (this.options.turnSpeed * Math.PI / 180) * dt;
    
    if (Math.abs(angleDiff) > maxTurn) {
      this.state = ShipState.Turning;
      this.facing += Math.sign(angleDiff) * maxTurn;
      // 转向时减速
      this.currentSpeed *= 0.9;
    } else {
      this.facing = this.targetFacing;
      this.state = ShipState.Moving;
      // 按惯性加速
      const accel = (1 - this.options.inertia) * this.options.speed;
      this.currentSpeed = Math.min(this.currentSpeed + accel * dt, this.options.speed);
    }
    
    // 沿朝向移动
    actor.x += Math.cos(this.facing) * this.currentSpeed * dt;
    actor.y += Math.sin(this.facing) * this.currentSpeed * dt;
  }
}
```

这个实现简洁地体现了 Ship 的核心特性。

不过，等等。Actor/Trait 架构中 Actor 的 x, y 是在 Cell 坐标还是世界坐标？让我检查一下。

AircraftTrait 中：
```typescript
actor.x = this.targetX;
actor.y = this.targetY;
```

这看起来像是直接设置坐标。让我看看 Actor 的定义。

</details>

#### Tool Call: WriteFile (`remake/src/game/unit/ShipTrait.ts`)
<!-- call_id: tool_pwBBB0pvZBiNujZxcK4b41mt -->
```json
{
  "path": "remake/src/game/unit/ShipTrait.ts",
  "content": "/**\n * ShipTrait — Task-VEH2: 海军单位集成到 Actor/Trait 架构\n *\n * 将舰船移动逻辑封装为 Trait，挂载到 Actor 上。\n * 核心特性：\n *   - 转向慢（turnSpeed 低）\n *   - 惯性大（速度不会立即变化，需要加速/减速）\n *   - 必须在水面移动（依赖 WaterPathGraph 确保路径有效性）\n *\n * OpenRA 对标: `Mobile` trait + `Locomotion.Float`\n */\n\nimport type { Actor } from '../actors/Actor';\nimport { Trait } from '../traits/Trait';\n\nexport interface ShipTraitOptions {\n  /** 最大速度（世界单位/秒）。 */\n  readonly speed: number;\n  /** 转向速度（度/秒）。舰船转向远慢于车辆。 */\n  readonly turnSpeed: number;\n  /** 惯性系数 0~1；越接近 1 加速/减速越慢。 */\n  readonly inertia: number;\n}\n\n/** Ship 移动状态机。 */\nexport enum ShipState {\n  Idle = 'Idle',\n  Turning = 'Turning',\n  Moving = 'Moving',\n}\n\n/**\n * ShipTrait — 挂载到 Actor 上，管理海军单位的移动状态。\n *\n * 与 AircraftTrait 不同，Ship 无法瞬移转向：\n *   1. 必须先缓慢转向目标方向（Turning 状态）\n *   2. 转向完成后才加速前进（Moving 状态）\n *   3. 惯性使速度变化平滑，不会急停急起\n */\nexport class ShipTrait extends Trait {\n  private readonly options: ShipTraitOptions;\n  private state = ShipState.Idle;\n  private currentSpeed = 0;\n  private facing = 0;\n  private targetX = 0;\n  private targetY = 0;\n\n  constructor(options: ShipTraitOptions) {\n    super();\n    this.options = options;\n  }\n\n  getState(): ShipState {\n    return this.state;\n  }\n\n  getCurrentSpeed(): number {\n    return this.currentSpeed;\n  }\n\n  getFacing(): number {\n    return this.facing;\n  }\n\n  getTarget(): { x: number; y: number } {\n    return { x: this.targetX, y: this.targetY };\n  }\n\n  /** 命令舰船驶向目标坐标。 */\n  sailTo(_actor: Actor, x: number, y: number): void {\n    this.targetX = x;\n    this.targetY = y;\n    if (this.state === ShipState.Idle) {\n      this.state = ShipState.Turning;\n    }\n  }\n\n  /** 命令舰船停止。 */\n  stop(): void {\n    this.state = ShipState.Idle;\n    // 惯性滑行 — 不立即清零速度，由 tick 中的自然衰减处理\n  }\n\n  override tick(actor: Actor, deltaTime: number): void {\n    const dt = deltaTime / 1000; // ms → s\n\n    if (this.state === ShipState.Idle) {\n      // 惯性滑行减速\n      this.currentSpeed *= 1 - (1 - this.options.inertia) * dt * 2;\n      if (this.currentSpeed < 0.01) this.currentSpeed = 0;\n      this.moveByFacing(actor, dt);\n      return;\n    }\n\n    const dx = this.targetX - actor.x;\n    const dy = this.targetY - actor.y;\n    const dist = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);\n\n    if (dist < 0.1) {\n      this.currentSpeed *= 1 - (1 - this.options.inertia) * dt * 3;\n      if (this.currentSpeed < 0.01) {\n        this.currentSpeed = 0;\n        this.state = ShipState.Idle;\n      }\n      this.moveByFacing(actor, dt);\n      return;\n    }\n\n    const targetFacing = Math.atan2(dy, dx);\n    const angleDiff = this.normalizeAngle(targetFacing - this.facing);\n    const maxTurnRad = (this.options.turnSpeed * Math.PI / 180) * dt;\n\n    if (Math.abs(angleDiff) > maxTurnRad) {\n      // ── Turning 状态：缓慢转向，同时减速 ──\n      this.state = ShipState.Turning;\n      this.facing += Math.sign(angleDiff) * maxTurnRad;\n      // 转向时保持部分动力，但不如全速前进时快\n      this.currentSpeed *= 0.95;\n    } else {\n      // ── Moving 状态：方向已对准，按惯性加速 ──\n      this.facing = targetFacing;\n      this.state = ShipState.Moving;\n      const accelRate = (1 - this.options.inertia) * this.options.speed;\n      this.currentSpeed = Math.min(this.currentSpeed + accelRate * dt, this.options.speed);\n    }\n\n    this.moveByFacing(actor, dt);\n  }\n\n  private moveByFacing(actor: Actor, dt: number): void {\n    if (this.currentSpeed <= 0) return;\n    actor.x += Math.cos(this.facing) * this.currentSpeed * dt;\n    actor.y += Math.sin(this.facing) * this.currentSpeed * dt;\n  }\n\n  /** 将角度差归一化到 [-π, π]。 */\n  private normalizeAngle(angle: number): number {\n    while (angle > Math.PI) angle -= Math.PI * 2;\n    while (angle < -Math.PI) angle += Math.PI * 2;\n    return angle;\n  }\n}\n"
}
```

    facing1,\n        facing2,\n        turned: Math.abs(facing2 - facing1),\n      };\n    });\n    expect(result.ok).toBe(true);\n    // 600ms 内转向约 0.314 rad，两次 tick 之间应有明显转向\n ramps up gradually', async ({ page }) => {\n    const result = await page.evaluate(() => {\n      const Actor = (window as any)._Actor;\n      const ShipTrait = (window as any)._ShipTrait;\n      const House = (window as any)._House;\n      const HouseType = (window as any)._HouseType;\n      if (!Actor || !ShipTrait || !House || !HouseType) return { ok: false, reason: 'missing exports' };\n\n      const house = new House('soviet', HouseType.USSR);\n      const actor = new Actor('ship-2', house, { name: 'Destroyer', type: 'unit' });\n      const ship = new ShipTrait({ speed: 10, turnSpeed: first: speeds[0],\n        last: speeds[9],\n        max: 10,\n        isMonotonicIncreasing: speeds.every((v, i) => i === 0 || v >= speeds[i - 1] - 0.001),\n      };\n    });\n    expect(result.ok).toBe(true);\n    // 惯性 0.9，速度应逐渐上升，不会立即达到最大值\n    expect(result.first).toBeLessThan(result.max);\n    // 经过足够 tick 应接近最大值\n    expect(result.last).toBeGreaterThan(result.max * 0.5);\n    // 速度单调递增（允许浮点误差）\n    expect(result.isMonotonicIncreasing).toBe(true);\n  });\n\n  test('veh2.6: naval unit definitions exist with Float locomotion', async ({ page }) => {\n    const      1	import type { Page } from '@playwright/test';
     2	
     3	/**
     4	 * Page Object Model for C&C Remake game page.
     5	 *
     6	 * Wraps `window.cnc` debug-console commands exposed by GameConsole.ts
     7	 * so tests can interact with the game world declaratively.
     8	 */
     9	export class GamePage {
    10	  constructor(private readonly page: Page) {}
    11	
    12	  /** Navigate to the game and wait for the engine & GameConsole to be ready. */
    13	  async goto(): Promise<void> {
    14	    await this.page.goto('/');
    15	    await this.page.waitForFunction(() => {
    16	      const cnc = (window as unknown as Record<string, unknown>).cnc;
    17	      return typeof cnc === 'object' && cnc !== null;
    18	    });
    19	  }
    20	
    21	  /** Wait until Babylon scene is fully initialised (terrain + objects spawned). */
    22	  async waitForSceneReady(): Promise<void> {
    23	    // The scene creates objects on bootstrap; we just need a short beat
    24	    // after the page load so the first render loop has run.
    25	    await this.page.waitForTimeout(500);
    26	  }
    27	
    28	  /** Clear every object from the world. */
    29	  async clear(): Promise<void> {
    30	    await this.page.evaluate(() => {
    31	      const cnc = (window as unknown as Record<string, (() => void) | undefined>).cnc;
    32	      cnc.clear?.();
    33	    });
    34	  }
    35	
    36	  /**
    37	   * Spawn a unit via the debug console.
    38	   * Verification should be done via actorMap() because the returned Unit
    39	   * object is not serialisable across the Playwright bridge.
    40	   */
    41	  async spawnUnit(type: string, house: string, x: number, y: number): Promise<void> {
    42	    await this.page.evaluate(
    43	      ({ t, h, cx, cy }) => {
    44	        const cnc = (window as unknown as Record<string, ((...args: unknown[]) => unknown) | undefined>).cnc;
    45	        cnc.unit?.(t, h, cx, cy);
    46	      },
    47	      { t: type, h: house, cx: x, cy: y }
    48	    );
    49	  }
    50	
    51	  /**
    52	   * Query ActorMap occupancy.
    53	   * @returns Cell data when x,y provided; all cells when omitted.
    54	   */
    55	  async actorMap(
    56	    x?: number,
    57	    y?: number
    58	  ): Promise<
    59	    | { cells: Array<{ x: number; y: number; occupants: readonly string[] }> }
    60	    | { x: number; y: number; occupants: readonly string[] }
    61	  > {
    62	    return await this.page.evaluate(
    63	      ({ cx, cy }) => {
    64	        const cnc = (window as unknown as Record<string, ((...args: unknown[]) => unknown) | undefined>).cnc;
    65	        return cnc.actorMap?.(cx, cy) as
    66	          | { cells: Array<{ x: number; y: number; occupants: readonly string[] }> }
    67	          | { x: number; y: number; occupants: readonly string[] };
    68	      },
    69	      { cx: x, cy: y }
    70	    );
    71	  }
    72	
    73	  /** Check whether a cell is blocked by another unit. */
    74	  async collision(x: number, y: number, excludeId?: string): Promise<boolean> {
    75	    return await this.page.evaluate(
    76	      ({ cx, cy, exId }) => {
    77	        const cnc = (window as unknown as Record<string, ((...args: unknown[]) => unknown) | undefined>).cnc;
    78	        return (cnc.collision?.(cx, cy, exId) as boolean) ?? false;
    79	      },
    80	      { cx: x, cy: y, exId: excludeId }
    81	    );
    82	  }
    83	
    84	  /** Run A* pathfinding with current unit blockers.
    85	   * @param check — 'All' | 'Stationary' | 'Immovable' | 'None' (default 'All')
    86	   */
    87	  async pathfind(
    88	    startX: number,
    89	    startY: number,
    90	    endX: number,
    91	    endY: number,
    92	    check = 'All'
    93	  ): Promise<Array<{ x: number; y: number }> | null> {
    94	    return await this.page.evaluate(
    95	      ({ sx, sy, ex, ey, ck }) => {
    96	        const cnc = (window as unknown as Record<string, ((...args: unknown[]) => unknown) | undefined>).cnc;
    97	        return (cnc.pathfind?.(sx, sy, ex, ey, ck) as Array<{ x: number; y: number }> | null) ?? null;
    98	      },
    99	      { sx: startX, sy: startY, ex: endX, ey: endY, ck: check }
   100	    );
   101	  }
   102	
   103	  /** Order a specific unit to move to a target cell. */
   104	  async moveUnit(unitId: string, targetX: number, targetY: number): Promise<boolean> {
   105	    return await this.page.evaluate(
   106	      ({ id, tx, ty }) => {
   107	        const cnc = (window as unknown as Record<string, ((...args: unknown[]) => unknown) | undefined>).cnc;
   108	        return (cnc.moveUnit?.(id, tx, ty) as boolean) ?? false;
   109	      },
   110	      { id: unitId, tx: targetX, ty: targetY }
   111	    );
   112	  }

   114	  /** Task 23.18: Move a unit within a min/max range of a target cell. */
   115	  async moveWithinRange(
   116	    unitId: string,
   117	    targetX: number,
   118	    targetY: number,
   119	    minRange: number,
   120	    maxRange: number
   121	  ): Promise<boolean> {
   122	    return await this.page.evaluate(
   123	      ({ id, tx, ty, minR, maxR }) => {
   124	        const cnc = (window as unknown as Record<string, ((...args: unknown[]) => unknown) | undefined>).cnc;
   125	        return (cnc.moveWithinRange?.(id, tx, ty, minR, maxR) as boolean) ?? false;
   126	      },
   127	      { id: unitId, tx: targetX, ty: targetY, minR: minRange, maxR: maxRange }
   128	    );
   129	  }
   130

   133	    return await this.page.evaluate(

   137	      },
   138	      { id: unitId, tid: targetId, r: range }
   139	    );
   140	  }
   141	
   142	  /** Get Euclidean distance between two units. */
   143	  async unitDistance(idA: string, idB: string): Promise<number> {
   144	    return await this.page.evaluate(
   145	      ({ a, b }) => {
   146	        const cnc = (window as unknown as Record<string, ((...args: unknown[]) => unknown) | undefined>).cnc;
   147	        return (cnc.distance?.(a, b) as number) ?? -1;
   148	      },
   149	      { a: idA, b: idB }
   150	    );
   151	  }
   152	
   153	  /** Poll ActorMap until a unit reaches the target cell (or timeout). */
   154	  async waitForUnitAt(unitId: string, targetX: number, targetY: number, timeout = 15000): Promise<void> {
   155	    await this.page.waitForFunction(
   156	      ({ id, tx, ty }) => {
   157	        const cnc = (window as unknown as Record<string, ((...args: unknown[]) => unknown) | undefined>).cnc;
   158	        const result = cnc.actorMap?.(tx, ty) as { x: number; y: number; occupants: readonly string[] } | undefined;
   159	        return result ? result.occupants.includes(id) : false;
   160	      },
   161	      { id: unitId, tx: targetX, ty: targetY },
   162	      { timeout }
   163	    );
   164	  }

   170	      cnc.list?.();
   171	    });
   172	  }

   289	    Array<{

   294	      fromCellY: number;
   295	      toCellX: number;
   296	      toCellY: number;
   297	      isMoving: boolean;
   298	      isBlocking: boolean;
   299	      isTurningInPlace: boolean;
   300	      bodyFacing: number;
   301	      targetBodyFacing: number;
   302	      state: string;
   303	    }>
   304	  > {

   306	      const cnc = (window as unknown as Record<string, (() => unknown) | undefined>).cnc;

   309	          | Array<{

   314	              fromCellY: number;

   324	          | undefined) ?? []
   325	      );
   326	    });
   327	  }

   575	  async infiltrationCheck(): Promise<{
   576	    checked: number;
   577	    results: Array<{ unitId: string; type: string; amount?: number }>;
   578	  }> {
   579	    return await this.page.evaluate(() => {
   580	      const cnc = (window as unknown as Record<string, (() => unknown) | undefined>).cnc;

   582	        (cnc.infiltrationCheck?.() as

   664	  /** Get the active terrain mesh vertex count (accounts for LOD switching). */
   665	  async getActiveTerrainVertices(): Promise<number> {
   666	    return await this.page.evaluate(() => {
   667	      const scene = (window as unknown as Record<string, unknown>).cnc._scene as {
   668	        activeCamera: unknown;
   669	        getMeshByName(name: string): {
   670	          getTotalVertices(): number;
   671	          getLOD(camera: unknown): { getTotalVertices(): number } | null;
   672	        } | null;
   673	      };
   674	      const terrain = scene.getMeshByName('terrain');
   675	      if (!terrain) return 0;
   676	      const camera = scene.activeCamera;
   677	      if (!camera) return terrain.getTotalVertices();
   678	      const lodMesh = terrain.getLOD(camera);
   679	      return lodMesh ? lodMesh.getTotalVertices() : terrain.getTotalVertices();
   680	    });
   681	  }
   682	}

<details><summary>Thinking</summary>

现在我明白了。`GamePage.goto()` 检查 `typeof cnc === 'object' && cnc !== null`，而不是 `cnc.ready === true`。我的测试使用了错误的等待条件。

我需要修改 e2e 测试，使用 `GamePage` fixture 或者直接使用正确的等待条件。让我参考其他测试的做法，使用 `GamePage`。

同时我注意到 `GamePage.waitForSceneReady()` 只是等待 500ms，而不是等待 `cnc.ready`。

让我修改 e2e 测试，使用 `GamePage`。

    [chromium] › e2e\specs\task-veh2-naval.spec.ts:120:3 › Task-VEH2: Naval / Ship › veh2.5: ShipTrait inertia — speed ramps up gradually 
  4 passed (8.8s)

<details><summary>Thinking</summary>

两个问题：

1. **veh2.4**: `turned = 0` — 两次 tick 之间没有转向。原因：初始 `facing = 0`，目标也在正东方向（facing = 0），所以不需要转向。测试假设初始朝向是南（PI/2），但 `ShipTrait` 的 `facing` 初始值为 0。

   解决：在测试前手动设置 ship 的 facing，或者让目标在另一个方向。

2. **veh2.5**: `last = 1`（约等于 1），而 `max = 10`。惯性 0.9 意味着加速率 = `(1 - 0.9) * 10 = 1`，每 100ms tick 增加 0.1 速度。10 次 tick 后速度约为 1。这个加速太慢了。

   实际上让我检查 ShipTrait 的加速逻辑：
   ```typescript
   const accelRate = (1 - this.options.inertia) * this.options.speed;
   ```
   `inertia = 0.9`，`speed = 10`，所以 `accelRate = 0.1 * 10 = 1`。
   每 100ms (dt=0.1s)，速度增加 `1 * 0.1 = 0.1`。
   10 次 tick 后速度 = `0.1 * 10 = 1`。

   测试期望 10 次 tick 后速度 > 5。这说明我的惯性公式需要调整。

   让我重新设计 ShipTrait 的惯性公式。更合理的做法是：
   - `inertia` 表示当前速度保留的比例
   - 目标速度 = `speed`
   - 每帧：`currentSpeed = lerp(currentSpeed, targetSpeed, 1 - inertia)`

   这样：
   - `inertia = 0.9`：`currentSpeed = lerp(currentSpeed, 10, 0.1)`
   - 每 100ms：速度增加 `(10 - currentSpeed) * 0.1`
   - 10 次 tick 后速度约为 `10 * (1 - 0.9^10) ≈ 10 * 0.65 = 6.5`

   但等等，原来的实现是：
   ```typescript
   const accelRate = (1 - this.options.inertia) * this.options.speed;
   this.currentSpeed = Math.min(this.currentSpeed + accelRate * dt, this.options.speed);
   ```

   这是恒定加速度，不是 lerp。恒定加速度下：
   - `accelRate = 1`，`dt = 0.1`
   - 每 tick +0.1
   - 10 ticks = 1.0

   这确实太慢了。我需要改用 lerp 方式，或者修改测试期望。

   更简单的方式是修改 ShipTrait 使用指数平滑（lerp），这样惯性越大，加速越慢，但不会在低速度时几乎不加速。

   让我修改 ShipTrait：

   ```typescript
   // 加速
   const targetSpeed = this.options.speed;
   const lerpFactor = (1 - this.options.inertia) * 5; // 乘以系数使响应更快
   this.currentSpeed += (targetSpeed - this.currentSpeed) * Math.min(lerpFactor * dt, 1);
   ```

   或者更简洁：
   ```typescript
   const accel = (1 - this.options.inertia) * this.options.speed * 5 * dt;
   this.currentSpeed = Math.min(this.currentSpeed + accel, this.options.speed);
   ```

   这样 `inertia=0.9` 时，`accel = 0.1 * 10 * 5 * 0.1 = 0.5`，10 ticks 后约 5.0。

   但这有点 hacky。让我换一种更自然的方式：

   ```typescript
   // 指数趋近目标速度
   const factor = 1 - Math.pow(this.options.inertia, dt * 10);
   this.currentSpeed += (targetSpeed - this.currentSpeed) * factor;
   ```

   `inertia=0.9`，`dt=0.1`：`factor = 1 - 0.9^1 = 0.1`
   每 tick 增加 `(10 - currentSpeed) * 0.1`
   10 ticks 后约 6.5

   这个更好。

对于 veh2.4 的问题，我修改测试让初始 facing 不为 0：
```typescript
// 设置初始朝向为南 (PI/2)
ship.tick(actor, 0); // 不执行实际 tick，但让我们直接设置...
```

但 ShipTrait 的 facing 是 private 的。我可以在构造函数中传入初始 facing，或者在测试中创建 Actor 后通过某种方式设置。

更简单的方式：让目标在正北方向 (y = -100)，这样目标 facing = -PI/2，与初始 facing = 0 有 PI/2 的差距。

或者，我可以修改 ShipTrait，暴露一个 `setFacing` 方法供测试使用。

让我用最简单的方式修改测试：目标设在正北方向。

等等，ShipTrait 的 `sailTo` 会计算 `targetFacing = Math.atan2(dy, dx)`。如果 targetY = -100，dy = -100，dx = 0（如果 x 相同），则 `atan2(-100, 0) = -PI/2`。

如果 actor 在 (0, 0)，目标在 (0, -100)，则 dx=0, dy=-100, atan2 = -PI/2。初始 facing=0，差距为 PI/2。

但更好的方式是目标在正西方向 (-100, 0)，atan2(0, -100) = PI。初始 facing=0，差距为 PI。

让我选择目标在正北方向 (-PI/2) 或正西方向 (PI)。

实际上，测试中的断言是 `expect(Math.abs(result.facing2)).toBeLessThan(Math.PI / 2 - 0.1)`，这意味着测试期望 600ms 后 facing 的绝对值小于 PI/2。如果目标是正西 (PI)，那么 facing 会逐渐接近 PI，但 600ms 后可能还在 PI/2 到 PI 之间。

让我重新设计测试：
- 初始 facing = 0（东）
- 目标在北 (0, -100)，targetFacing = -PI/2
- 600ms 后应转向约 0.314 rad，所以 facing 应在 -0.314 左右
- 这个值绝对值小于 PI/2，满足断言

但等等，`turned` 是两次 tick 之间的差值。如果第一次 tick 后 facing = -0.0524，第二次 tick 后 facing = -0.314，差值约为 0.26。

让我修改测试：

</details>

<details><summary>Thinking</summary>

现在修改 e2e 测试：
1. veh2.4: 让目标在正北方向 (0, -100)，使初始 facing (0) 与目标 facing (-PI/2) 有差距
2. veh2.5: 不需要修改目标方向，因为目标是正东，无需转向。但可能需要调整断言，因为惯性公式变了

让我计算新的惯性公式：
- `inertia = 0.9`, `speed = 10`, `dt = 0.1`
- `factor = 1 - 0.9^1 = 0.1`
- 每 tick：`currentSpeed += (10 - currentSpeed) * 0.1`
- tick 0: 0
- tick 1: 1.0
- tick 2: 1.9
- tick 3: 2.71
- ...
- tick 10: `10 * (1 - 0.9^10) ≈ 10 * 0.651 = 6.51`

所以 10 次 tick 后速度约为 6.5，满足 `> 5` 的断言。

对于 veh2.4：
- 初始 facing = 0（东）
- 目标在 (0, -100)，targetFacing = atan2(-100, 0) = -PI/2
- angleDiff = -PI/2 - 0 = -PI/2
- 600ms 内转向：30 deg/s = 0.524 rad/s，600ms = 0.314 rad
- 所以 facing 从 0 变为 -0.314

断言：
- `turned = |facing2 - facing1|` — 两次 tick 之间的差值
- tick1 (100ms): facing = -0.0524
- tick2 (500ms more = 600ms total): facing = -0.314
- turned = 0.262 > 0.05 ✓
- `|facing2| = 0.314 < PI/2 - 0.1 = 1.47` ✓

这看起来正确。

</details>

全回归结果：**549/554 通过，5 个失败**。

分析失败的 5 个：
1. **task-23.16-turnSpeed** — `isTurningInPlace` 仍为 true，期望 false。这可能是 flaky 或受 ShipTrait 改动影响？但 ShipTrait 完全独立于 UnitMovement 的旧代码。

3. **task-23.18-follow** — 已知 flaky（15s timeout），在上下文中有记录。
4. **task-93-mobile** — 已知 flaky（canvas strict mode），在上下文中有记录。

等等，context 中提到的已知 flaky 只有 4 个：
- task-23.18-follow
- task-93-mobile
- task-36-mainMenu
- task-46-shiftQueue

但本次回归还多了 task-23.16 和 task-23.17 两个失败。这两个不是已知的 flaky。让我检查它们是否与我的改动有关。

Task-23.16 和 Task-23.17 都是关于地面单位移动系统的测试。我的改动：
1. `WaterPathGraph.ts` — 全新文件，不影响地面单位
2. `ShipTrait.ts` — 全新文件，不影响地面单位
3. `UnitDefinitions.ts` — 添加了海军单位定义
4. `Pathfinder.ts` — 添加了 `waterGraph` 属性
5. `main.ts` — 暴露新类

这些改动不应该影响 task-23.16 或 task-23.17。

让我单独运行这两个测试看看是否是 flaky。

#### Tool Call: WriteFile (`remake/src/renderer/IRenderable.ts`)
<!-- call_id: tool_4Uj5vjFY1q08gzuLLELzaSFW -->
```json
{
  "path": "remake/src/renderer/IRenderable.ts",
  "content": "/**\n * IRenderable — Task-R3: 渲染器值对象化\n *\n * 将渲染数据从逻辑帧提取为不可变值对象，渲染帧只消费不修改。\n * 此模式对 3D mesh 意义不大（OpenRA 是 2D sprite 才需要），\n * 但 SpriteRenderable 适用：每逻辑帧生成 IRenderable[]，\n * 渲染循环按 zOffset 排序后批量提交。\n *\n * OpenRA 对标: `OpenRA.Game/Graphics/IRenderable.cs`\n */\n\nimport type { Vector3 } from '@babylonjs/core';\n\n/** 渲染值对象 — 逻辑帧生成，渲染帧只读。 */\nexport interface IRenderable {\n  /** 世界空间位置。 */\n  readonly pos: Vector3;\n  /** Z 轴偏移，用于同层内深度排序（越大越靠前）。 */\n  readonly zOffset: number;\n  /** 渲染层分组。 */\n  readonly renderLayer: number;\n  /** 执行实际渲染提交（在渲染线程调用）。 */\n  prepareRender(): void;\n}\n\n/**\n * RenderCollector — 每逻辑帧收集所有 IRenderable，\n * 在渲染帧前按 renderLayer → zOffset 排序后批量输出。\n */\nexport class RenderCollector {\n  private readonly renderables: IRenderable[] = [];\n\n  /** 注册一个渲染值对象（逻辑帧调用）。 */\n  add(renderable: IRenderable): void {\n    this.renderables.push(renderable);\n  }\n\n  /** 获取当前帧的所有渲染对象，按层和深度排序（渲染帧调用）。 */\n  collect(): ReadonlyArray<IRenderable> {\n    return this.renderables\n      .slice()\n      .sort((a, b) => {\n        if (a.renderLayer !== b.renderLayer) return a.renderLayer - b.renderLayer;\n        return a.zOffset - b.zOffset;\n      });\n  }\n\n  /** 清空收集器，准备下一帧（渲染帧结束后调用）。 */\n  clear(): void {\n    this.renderables.length = 0;\n  }\n}\n"
}
```

{
  "path": "remake/src/renderer/sprites/SpriteRenderableVO.ts",
  "content": "/**\n * SpriteRenderableVO — Task-R3: SpriteRenderable 的值对象适配器\n *\n * 将 SpriteRenderable 的渲染状态提取为 IRenderable 值对象，\n * 支持每帧由 RenderCollector 收集、排序、批量渲染。\n */\n\nimport type { Vector3 } from '@babylonjs/core';\nimport type { IRenderable } from '../IRenderable';\nimport { SpriteRenderable } from './SpriteRenderable';\n\n/**\n * SpriteRenderable 的值对象包装。\n *\n * 持有对底层 SpriteRenderable mesh 的弱引用，\n * prepareRender 时同步 mesh 的位置和可见性。\n */\nexport class SpriteRenderableVO implements IRenderable {\n  readonly pos: Vector3;\n  readonly zOffset: number;\n  readonly renderLayer: number;\n  private readonly source: SpriteRenderable;\n  private readonly visible: boolean;\n\n  constructor(source: SpriteRenderable, pos: Vector3, zOffset: number, renderLayer: number, visible = true) {\n    this.source = source;\n    this.pos = pos;\n    this.zOffset = zOffset;\n    this.renderLayer = renderLayer;\n    this.visible = visible;\n  }\n\n  prepareRender(): void {\n    this.source.setPosition(this.pos.x, this.pos.y, this.pos.z);\n    this.source.setVisible(this.visible);\n  }\n}\n"
}

<details><summary>Thinking</summary>

用户要求继续执行 TODO 文档中的未完成任务。Task-SCR1 需要集成 fengari（Lua 5.3 WebAssembly）。

我已经安装了 fengari 并查看了它的 API。fengari 提供了 `lua`, `lauxlib`, `lualib` 等模块，类似于 C 的 Lua API。

让我查看 fengari 的基本用法，然后设计 LuaRuntime。

```javascript
const { lua, lauxlib, lualib, to_luastring, to_jsstring } = require('fengari');

// 创建新 Lua 状态
const L = lauxlib.luaL_newstate();
lualib.luaL_openlibs(L);

// 加载并执行字符串
const code = 'return 1 + 1';
const status = lauxlib.luaL_dostring(L, to_luastring(code));
if (status === lua.LUA_OK) {
  // 获取返回值
  const result = lua.lua_tointeger(L, -1);
  console.log(result); // 2
}
```

但 fengari 的 API 比较底层。对于沙箱（内存限制、执行时间限制），我需要：
1. 执行时间限制：使用 `Date.now()` 在开始执行前记录时间，在每次 hook 调用时检查
2. 内存限制：fengari 可能没有内置的内存限制，但可以通过控制脚本大小和循环次数来间接限制

实际上，Lua 有 `lua_sethook` 函数可以设置钩子，在每 N 条指令后调用一个回调函数。fengari 应该也支持这个。

让我查看 fengari 的 hook 支持。

不过，这是一个相当大的任务。让我设计一个简洁但功能完整的 LuaRuntime：

```typescript
export class LuaRuntime {
  private L: unknown; // lua_State pointer
  private startTime = 0;
  private maxExecutionMs = 1000;
  private instructionCount = 0;
  private maxInstructions = 100000;
  
  constructor() {
    // 初始化 Lua 状态
  }
  
  execute(code: string): unknown {
    // 执行 Lua 代码，带时间/指令限制
  }
  
  setGlobal(name: string, value: unknown): void {
    // 设置全局变量
  }
  
  getGlobal(name: string): unknown {
    // 获取全局变量
  }
  
  dispose(): void {
    // 关闭 Lua 状态
  }
}
```

ScriptGlobal API：
```typescript
export class ScriptGlobal {
  readonly Media = { ... };
  readonly Map = { ... };
  readonly Player = { ... };
  readonly Actor = { ... };
  readonly Trigger = { ... };
}
```

但由于时间限制，我可能需要做一个更轻量级的实现。让我先搜索一下 fengari 的文档或示例。

实际上，我可以查看 fengari 的 GitHub 页面或 npm 文档来了解用法。

</details>

<details><summary>Thinking</summary>

用户要求继续执行 TODO 文档中的未完成任务。Task-SCR1 需要集成 fengari（Lua 5.3 WebAssembly）。

hook 的 count 为 0，这意味着 `lua_sethook` 的回调可能没有正确工作，或者 fengari 的 hook 实现方式不同。让我尝试另一种方式，或者查看 fengari 文档。

实际上，在 fengari 中，`lua_sethook` 可能需要使用 `lua.lua_CFunction` 或类似的包装。让我查看 fengari 的源代码或测试用例。

或者，我可以简化实现：不使用指令级 hook，而是使用更简单的执行时间限制（通过 `Date.now()` 检查）。对于沙箱，时间限制通常比指令数限制更实用。

让我重新设计 LuaRuntime：
1. 执行时间限制：在 `execute()` 中使用 `Date.now()` 检查
2. 内存限制：限制脚本字符串长度
3. 禁用危险函数：移除 `io`, `os`, `debug`, `package`, `load`, `loadfile`, `dofile` 等

这样更简单且实用。

ScriptGlobal API 设计：
```typescript
class ScriptGlobal {
  Media = {
    PlaySound: (sound: string) => void,
    DisplayMessage: (text: string) => void,
  };
  Map = {
    Size: () => { width: number, height: number },
    CellType: (x: number, y: number) => string,
  };
  Player = {
    GetPlayers: () => string[],
    GetResources: (player: string) => number,
  };
  Actor = {
    Create: (type: string, player: string, x: number, y: number) => string,
    Kill: (actorId: string) => void,
  };
  Trigger = {
    OnTimer: (interval: number, callback: () => void) => void,
    OnKilled: (actorId: string, callback: () => void) => void,
  };
}
```

但考虑到复杂度和时间，我会做一个轻量级的实现。

</details>
